                    addressBookUrl: '/webapp/wcs/stores/servlet/AddressBookForm?catalogId=12051&langId=-20&storeId=10151'
                
            };
            var header = new Header(options);
            header.update();
        };
        SystemHelper.addLoader(loader);
    });

<script type="text/javascript">    
        require(["okey/modules/shopcart/MiniShoppingCart", "okey/utils/SystemHelper"], function(MiniShoppingCart, SystemHelper) {
           var loader = function() {
                var settings = {                 	                   
                    storeId: 10151,                    
                    cartContentsElementId: "MiniShoppingCartContents",
                    totalElementId: "miniShopCartTotal",
                    countElementId: "miniShopCartSum",
                    stickerTotalElementId: "miniShopCartStickerTotal",
                    popupElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded",
                    qtyUomElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_qtyUom",
                    qtyElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_qty",
                    qtyTitleElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_qtyTitle",
                    priceElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_price",
                    priceTotalElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_orderTotal",
                    titleElementId: "MiniShopCartAddedProdImg_Title",
                    nameAndUrlElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_NameAndUrl",
                    imageElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_Image",

                    stickerInfoElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_stickerInfo",
                    specialPriceStickerElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_specialPriceSticker",
                    stickerQuantityElementId: "MiniShopCartProductAdded_stickerQuantity",

                    rootServerAddress: dojo.byId("MiniShoppingCart_rootServerAddressValue").innerHTML,
                    imageNoImage: dojo.byId("MiniShopCartProductAdded_NoImageHidden").innerHTML,
                    isDebug: false
                };

                var miniCart = new MiniShoppingCart(settings);
                if (!SystemHelper.checkCurrentPageByCodes("shopcart"))
                	miniCart.load();
            };
            SystemHelper.addLoader(loader);
        });

	require(["dojo/on"], function(on) {
		on(document, "a.facetbutton:click", function(event) {
			var checkbox = document.getElementById(this.getAttribute("data-for"));
			checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
			if (this.getAttribute("role") == "checkbox") {
				this.setAttribute("aria-checked", checkbox.checked);
			}
			checkbox.onclick();
			event.preventDefault();
	   });
	});
